<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непроизвольный.html>непроизво́льный</a> (8587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвольный.html>произво́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proizvólʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емый</a> (9574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nepronicájemyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impenetrable, impervious, impermeable, proof, tight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>зву́ка</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nepronicájemyj</b> dlja zvúka</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">soundproof</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nepronicájemyj</b> dlja vody</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">waterproof; watertight</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тьма.html>тьма</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nepronicájemaja</b> tʹma</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">pitch-darkness</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроницаемый.html>непроница́емая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йна</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nepronicájemaja</b> tájna</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">impenetrable/unfathomable mystery</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мый</a> (12366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проходить.html>проходи́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proxodímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neproxodímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impassable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neproxodímyj</b> les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">impenetrable forest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neproxodímaja</b> grjazʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">impassable mud</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> utter, rank, hopeless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neproxodímyj</b> durák</i> ― <span class="e-translation">perfect/utter fool</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непроходимый.html>непроходи́мое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:невежество.html>неве́жество</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neproxodímoje</b> nevéžestvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rank ignorance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***непрошеный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непрошеный.html>непро́шеный</a> (16754)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непрошеный.html>непро́шеный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nepróšenyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>uninvited, unasked-for, uncalled-for, unwanted, unwarranted, unsolicited, unbidden
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">непрошенный <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>гость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neprošennyj gostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">uninvited/unbidden guest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">непрошенный <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">neprošennyj sovét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">unasked-for/unsolicited/unwanted/uninvited advice</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неработающий.html>нерабо́тающий</a> (22885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работающий.html>рабо́тающий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótajuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неработающий.html>нерабо́тающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerabótajuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>idle, out of service/work</li>
<li>unemployed, out of work

***неразбериха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́ха</a> (13918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разбер-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razber-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sort out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, using the present-tense stem of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разобраться.html>разобра́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razobrátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; literally "thing that can't be sorted out".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerazberíxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразбериха.html>неразбери́х</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a> (8919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разборчивый.html>разбо́рчивый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbórčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerazbórčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>illegible, indecipherable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почерк.html>по́черк</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyj</b> póčerk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">indecipherable handwriting</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>inarticulate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyje</b> slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">inarticulate words</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>undemanding, undiscerning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неразборчивый.html>неразбо́рчивый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкус.html>вкус</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nerazbórčivyj</b> vkus</i> ― <span class="e-translation">undiscerning taste</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>unscrupulous, unprincipled</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неразговорчивый.html>неразгово́рчивый</a> (19357)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разговорчивый.html>разгово́рчивый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razgovórčivyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразговорчивый.html>неразгово́рчивый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerazgovórčivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>taciturn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">untalkative, silent</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрыв.html>разры́в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrýv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or perhaps <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разры́вный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrývnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>нерв</a> (2435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>нерв</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerv</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nerve</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нервировать.html>нерви́ровать</a> (24996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нервировать.html>нерви́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nervírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
